# Evolute Solutions — Memory / Operating Context

## TL;DR
Evolute Solutions sells Meta ads + AI follow-up (SMS) + appointment setting for home remodeling/construction companies. Primary operating surfaces: Discord (client comms + internal), Asana (task mgmt), Notion (docs/SOPs).

## Core offer
- **Offer:** Meta Ads → leads → AI follow-up systems to text and book appointments.
- **Win condition:** In-person appointments with qualified homeowners (not junk leads).
- **Pricing / collections:** typically ~$1.5k–$2k collected on the first call; backend revenue often brings total to ~$4k–$8k+ (sometimes >$10k). LTV not yet well-measured.
- **ICP:** established remodeling/construction company with budget to invest, good at closing, good communication.

## Acquisition channels (current)
- Primary: cold SMS.
- Also scaling: cold callers / appointment setter team.
- Paid ads: ~$100–$200/day; currently around breakeven; goal is to improve performance.

## Current bottlenecks
- Not enough calls per day.
- Too many unqualified calls ("broke people").

## Delivery lifecycle (high level)
1) Client signs → onboarding form + onboarding call in Discord.
2) Connect Meta assets / accounts.
3) Launch ads usually within ~1 week (or less).
4) Ongoing: monitor ads, communicate with client, iterate.

## Roles
- Appointment setters team.
- Closer: Max.
- CSM/Ops Manager: Davi (client success + operations).
- Media buyer: Meta Ads manager focus.

- **Guild/server id:** `1164939432722440282`

## Client Success Sweep (v1 checklist)
For each active client channel:
1) Have we talked to them within the last few days?
2) Is there something we need to respond to?
3) Since the last-touch point, scan the conversation for **executable actions** discussed (requested changes, complaints, promised follow-ups) and capture status/owner.
4) Results signal (no Meta API initially): are they happy / complaining / asking for changes?
5) Contract: warn only if **within 30 days**.
   - Source: Asana **CSM/Ops Task Management** board section `Contract Expire (date)` and the card's **due_on** (appears to be the end date).

## toolResult (2026-02-24T02:36:59.576Z)

#!/usr/bin/env python3
"""GHL Daily Appointments Fetch (read-only)

Purpose (step 1): reliably fetch the raw data needed for a daily appointment report.
- Identify the 2 target calendars by partial name match
- Fetch /calendars/events for a date window (default: today local tz)
- Print a simple rollup by calendar + status + (optionally) createdBy/assigned user

This script does NOT write anything to GHL.

Env vars:
- GHL_PRIVATE_INTEGRATION_TOKEN (or another Bearer token with the needed scopes)
- GHL_LOCATION_ID (Evolute Solutions Main)
Optional:
- GHL_BASE_URL (default: https://services.leadconnectorhq.com)

Usage:
  python3 scripts/ghl_daily_appointments.py \
    --tz America/Bogota \
    --date 2026-02-23

  # or date range:
  python3 scripts/ghl_daily_appointments.py --start 2026-02-23T00:00:00 --end 2026-02-24T00:00:00

Notes:
- The official docs confirm these endpoints exist:
  - GET /calendars/
  - GET /calendars/events
- Query params for /calendars/events vary; we will try common patterns and
  print the exact failure body if the API rejects them.
"""

from __future__ import annotations

import argparse
import datetime as dt
import json
import os
import sys
from zoneinfo import ZoneInfo

import requests

DEFAULT_BASE = "https://services.leadconnectorhq.com"
DEFAULT_VERSION = "2021-07-28"  # used by LeadConnector/HighLevel endpoints

CAL_MATCHES = {
    "meta": ["ai strategy session meta inbound", "meta inbound", "meta"],
    "cold": ["cold sms"],
}


def iso(dt_obj: dt.datetime) -> str:
    # always output ISO 8601 with timezone offset
    return dt_obj.isoformat()


def req(session: requests.Session, method: str, url: str, *, params=None, json_body=None):
    resp = session.request(method, url, params=params, json=json_body, timeout=60)
    text = resp.text
    try:
        body = resp.json() if text else None
    except Exception:
        body = text
    return resp.status_code, body


def find_calendars(calendars: list[dict]) -> dict[str, dict]:
    """Return mapping {meta: calendarObj, cold: calendarObj} based on fuzzy name contains."""
    out: dict[str, dict] = {}
    for cal in calendars:
        name = (cal.get("name") or "").strip().lower()
        for key, needles in CAL_MATCHES.items():
            if key in out:
                continue
            if any(n in name for n in needles):
                out[key] = cal
    return out


def main():
    ap = argparse.ArgumentParser()
    ap.add_argument("--base", default=os.getenv("GHL_BASE_URL", DEFAULT_BASE))
    ap.add_argument("--token", default=os.getenv("GHL_PRIVATE_INTEGRATION_TOKEN", ""))
    ap.add_argument("--location", default=os.getenv("GHL_LOCATION_ID", ""))
    ap.add_argument("--tz", default="America/Bogota")
    ap.add_argument("--date", help="Local date YYYY-MM-DD (build start/end as full day)")
    ap.add_argument("--start", help="ISO datetime")
    ap.add_argument("--end", help="ISO datetime")
    ap.add_argument("--dump", action="store_true", help="Dump raw events JSON to stdout")
    ap.add_argument("--out", default="", help="Write raw JSON output to this file path")
    args = ap.parse_args()

    if not args.token:
        print("Missing token: set GHL_PRIVATE_INTEGRATION_TOKEN", file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(2)
    if not args.location:
        print("Missing location: set GHL_LOCATION_ID", file=sys.stderr)
        sys.exit(2)

    tz = ZoneInfo(args.tz)

    if args.start and args.end:
        start = dt.datetime.fromisoformat(args.start)
        end = dt.datetime.fromisoformat(args.end)
    else:
        if not args.date:
            # default to today in tz
            today = dt.datetime.now(tz).date()
        else:
            today = dt.date.fromisoformat(args.date)
        start = dt.datetime(today.year, today.month, today.day, 0, 0, 0, tzinfo=tz)
        end = start + dt.timedelta(days=1)

    session = requests.Session()
    session.headers.update(
        {
            "Authorization": f"Bearer {args.token}",
            "Accept": "application/json",
            "Content-Type": "application/json",
            "Version": DEFAULT_VERSION,
        }
    )

    # 1) Calendars
    cal_url = f"{args.base}/calendars/"
    code, body = req(session, "GET", cal_url, params={"locationId": args.location})
    if code != 200:
        print("GET /calendars/ failed", code)
        print(json.dumps(body, indent=2) if not isinstance(body, str) else body)
        sys.exit(1)

    # Body shape can vary; try common wrappers
    calendars = None
    if isinstance(body, dict):
        for k in ("calendars", "items", "data"):
            if isinstance(body.get(k), list):
                calendars = body[k]
                break
    if calendars is None and isinstance(body, list):
        calendars = body
    if calendars is None:
        print("Unexpected /calendars response shape:")
        print(json.dumps(body, indent=2) if not isinstance(body, str) else body)
        sys.exit(1)

    picked = find_calendars(calendars)
    if "meta" not in picked or "cold" not in picked:
        # Print list for manual verification
        names = [
            {"id": c.get("id"), "name": c.get("name"), "teamId": c.get("teamId"), "locationId": c.get("locationId")}
            for c in calendars
        ]
        print("Could not confidently match both calendars. Found matches:")
        print(json.dumps({k: {"id": v.get("id"), "name": v.get("name")} for k, v in picked.items()}, indent=2))
        print("All calendars (id,name):")
        print(json.dumps(names, indent=2))
        sys.exit(1)

    cal_meta = picked["meta"]
    cal_cold = picked["cold"]

    # 2) Events
    events_url = f"{args.base}/calendars/events"

    # The docs don't show params in extracted text; we try a few known patterns.
    # Pattern A (common): calendarId + startTime/endTime
    attempts = []

    def try_params(label: str, params: dict):
        code, body = req(session, "GET", events_url, params=params)
        attempts.append((label, code, body))
        return code, body

    # Try meta calendar
    events: dict[str, list] = {}
    for cal_key, cal_obj in ("meta", cal_meta), ("cold", cal_cold):
        cal_id = cal_obj.get("id")
        if not cal_id:
            print(f"Calendar missing id for {cal_key}: {cal_obj}")
            sys.exit(1)

        # Try a few param names. We'll stop on first 200.
        variants = [
            ("startTime/endTime", {"locationId": args.location, "calendarId": cal_id, "startTime": iso(start), "endTime": iso(end)}),
            ("start/end", {"locationId": args.location, "calendarId": cal_id, "start": iso(start), "end": iso(end)}),
            ("from/to", {"locationId": args.location, "calendarId": cal_id, "from": iso(start), "to": iso(end)}),
        ]

        ok = False
        last = None
        for label, params in variants:
            code, body = try_params(f"{cal_key}:{label}", params)
            last = (code, body)
            if code == 200:
                ok = True
                break
        if not ok:
            print(f"GET /calendars/events failed for {cal_key} calendar ({cal_obj.get('name')})")
            for label, code, body in attempts[-len(variants):]:
                print(f"  attempt {label} -> {code}")
                preview = body
                if isinstance(preview, dict) and len(json.dumps(preview)) > 2000:
                    # trim
                    preview = {"keys": list(preview.keys())}
                print("   ", json.dumps(preview, indent=2) if not isinstance(preview, str) else preview[:500])
            sys.exit(1)

        # Parse items
        items = None
        if isinstance(body, dict):
            for k in ("events", "items", "data"):
                if isinstance(body.get(k), list):
                    items = body[k]
                    break
        if items is None and isinstance(body, list):
            items = body
        if items is None:
            print(f"Unexpected /calendars/events response shape for {cal_key}:")
            print(json.dumps(body, indent=2) if not isinstance(body, str) else body)
            sys.exit(1)
        events[cal_key] = items

    # 3) Rollup (minimal)
    def status_of(ev: dict) -> str:
        # We don't know the field yet; try common keys.
        for k in ("status", "appointmentStatus", "eventStatus", "confirmationStatus"):
            v = ev.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip():
                return v.strip()
        # some APIs use booleans
        if ev.get("confirmed") is True:
            return "confirmed"
        if ev.get("confirmed") is False:
            return "unconfirmed"
        return "(unknown)"

    def created_by_of(ev: dict) -> str:
        for k in ("createdBy", "createdById", "userId", "assignedUserId", "assignedTo", "ownerId"):
            v = ev.get(k)
            if isinstance(v, str) and v.strip():
                return v.strip()
            if isinstance(v, dict):
                # sometimes {id,name}
                if isinstance(v.get("id"), str):
                    return v.get("id")
        return "(unknown)"

    summary = {}
    for cal_key, items in events.items():
        by_status = {}
        by_creator = {}
        for ev in items:
            if not isinstance(ev, dict):
                continue
            st = status_of(ev)
            by_status[st] = by_status.get(st, 0) + 1
            cr = created_by_of(ev)
            by_creator[cr] = by_creator.get(cr, 0) + 1
        summary[cal_key] = {
            "calendar": {"id": (cal_meta if cal_key == "meta" else cal_cold).get("id"), "name": (cal_meta if cal_key == "meta" else cal_cold).get("name")},
            "count": len(items),
            "by_status": dict(sorted(by_status.items(), key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[0]))),
            "by_creator": dict(sorted(by_creator.items(), key=lambda x: (-x[1], x[0]))),
        }

    out_obj = {
        "window": {"start": iso(start), "end": iso(end), "tz": args.tz},
        "locationId": args.location,
        "calendars": {
            "meta": {"id": cal_meta.get("id"), "name": cal_meta.get("name")},
            "cold": {"id": cal_cold.get("id"), "name": cal_cold.get("name")},
        },
        "summary": summary,
        "raw": events if args.dump else None,
    }

    if args.out:
        os.makedirs(os.path.dirname(args.out), exist_ok=True)
        with open(args.out, "w", encoding="utf-8") as f:
            json.dump(out_obj, f, indent=2)
        print(f"Wrote {args.out}")
    else:
        # print summary only
        print(json.dumps({k: v for k, v in out_obj.items() if k != "raw"}, indent=2))


if __name__ == "__main__":
    main()
